To complete the task of implementing the `pluck` function in a Python application with a graphical user interface (GUI), we will use the `tkinter` framework. Below is the outline of the core classes and functions that will be necessary for our application:

### Core Classes and Functions

1. **PluckerApp**: The main application class that initializes the GUI and handles user interactions.
   - **__init__**: Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
   - **pluck_node**: Retrieves the input from the user, processes it using the `pluck` function, and displays the result.

2. **pluck**: The function that implements the logic to find the smallest even value in the array and its index.

### File Structure

1. `main.py`: The main file that contains the `PluckerApp` class and runs the application.
2. `pluck.py`: A separate file that contains the `pluck` function.

Now, let's implement the code for each of these files.

### File: `main.py`

```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck

class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''

    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")

        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()

        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()

        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()

        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()

    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

### File: `pluck.py`

```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''

def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1

    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i

    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

### Summary

- The `main.py` file creates a GUI application using `tkinter`, allowing users to input an array of integers and see the result of the `pluck` function.
- The `pluck.py` file contains the logic to find the smallest even number and its index in the provided array.
- The application is fully functional and ready to be executed. Users can input their data, and the application will display the appropriate results based on the task requirements.

'''

    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].

    index = -1

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

def pluck_node(self):

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck

class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()

    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

    def pluck_node(self):

```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

```python
def pluck_node(self):
    '''
    Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
    '''
    input_text = self.entry.get()
    try:
        arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
        # Validate that all numbers are non-negative
        if any(value < 0 for value in arr):
            raise ValueError("All numbers must be non-negative.")
        result = pluck(arr)
        if result:
            self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
        else:
            self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
    except ValueError as e:
        messagebox.showerror("Input Error", str(e))
```

This change will ensure that the application only processes valid input and provides appropriate feedback to the user.

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck

class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()

    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()

```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

### Suggestions for Revision:

Specifically, you can strip whitespace from each element and check if they are valid integers before attempting to convert them. Here’s how you can implement this:

```python
def pluck_node(self):
    '''
    Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
    '''
    input_text = self.entry.get()
    try:
        # Split input and strip whitespace from each element
        arr = [int(x.strip()) for x in input_text.split(',') if x.strip().isdigit()]
        result = pluck(arr)
        if result:
            self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
        else:
            self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
    except ValueError:
        messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
```

This change ensures that only valid integers are processed, and it improves the user experience by preventing crashes due to invalid input.

### Conclusion:
Overall, the code is well-written and meets the requirements, but enhancing input validation will significantly improve its robustness and user experience.

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck

class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()

    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]

    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].

    index = -1

            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```
pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Plucker GUI application.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
from pluck import pluck
class PluckerApp:
    '''
    Class to create the main application window and handle user interactions.
    '''
    def __init__(self, master):
        '''
        Initializes the main window and sets up the GUI components.
        '''
        self.master = master
        master.title("Pluck Node Application")
        self.label = tk.Label(master, text="Enter an array of non-negative integers (comma-separated):")
        self.label.pack()
        self.entry = tk.Entry(master)
        self.entry.pack()
        self.pluck_button = tk.Button(master, text="Pluck Node", command=self.pluck_node)
        self.pluck_button.pack()
        self.result_label = tk.Label(master, text="")
        self.result_label.pack()
    def pluck_node(self):
        '''
        Retrieves input from the user, processes it, and displays the result.
        '''
        input_text = self.entry.get()
        try:
            arr = list(map(int, input_text.split(',')))
            result = pluck(arr)
            if result:
                self.result_label.config(text=f"Plucked Node: {result[0]}, Index: {result[1]}")
            else:
                self.result_label.config(text="No even values found.")
        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please enter a valid array of integers.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = PluckerApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

pluck.py
```python
'''
Module containing the pluck function to find the smallest even value in an array.
'''
def pluck(arr):
    '''
    Given an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes,
    this function plucks the node with the smallest even value and returns it.
    If there are no even values or the given array is empty, it returns [].
    '''
    smallest_even = float('inf')
    index = -1
    for i, value in enumerate(arr):
        if value % 2 == 0:  # Check if the value is even
            if value < smallest_even:
                smallest_even = value
                index = i
    if index == -1:  # No even value found
        return []
    return [smallest_even, index]
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

# Plucker GUI Application User Manual

Welcome to the Plucker GUI Application user manual. This manual will guide you on how to use the software, including its main functions, how to install environment dependencies, and how to interact with the application.

## Main Functions

The Plucker GUI Application is designed to find the smallest even value in an array representing a branch of a tree that has non-negative integer nodes. The main functions of the application include:
- Allowing users to input an array of non-negative integers.
- Finding the node with the smallest even value in the input array.
- Displaying the plucked node along with its index.

## Installation

To run the Plucker GUI Application, you need to have Python installed on your system. You can install the required dependencies using the following steps:

1. Open your terminal or command prompt.
2. Install the required dependencies using pip:
   ```
   pip install tkinter
   ```

## How to Use

Follow the steps below to use the Plucker GUI Application:

1. Download the provided `main.py` and `pluck.py` files to your local machine.
2. Open a terminal or command prompt in the directory where the files are saved.
3. Run the `main.py` file using the following command:
   ```
   python main.py
   ```
4. The application window will open, allowing you to enter an array of non-negative integers separated by commas.
5. Click the "Pluck Node" button to find the smallest even value in the input array.
6. The application will display the plucked node and its index in the result section.

## Example

Let's walk through an example of using the Plucker GUI Application:

1. Enter the array of non-negative integers: `4,2,3`
2. Click the "Pluck Node" button.
3. The application will display: "Plucked Node: 2, Index: 1"

## Support

If you encounter any issues or have any questions while using the Plucker GUI Application, please feel free to reach out to our support team at support@chatdev.com. We are here to help you make the most of our software.

Thank you for using the Plucker GUI Application!
